INC-SOURCE (PHOTO) Rotary Uranium Target that is struck by an     2303900100028 
            electron beam with a mean energy of 105 MeV and an    2303900100029 
            average current of 70 uA. The neutron beam was        2303900100030 
            collimated before the fission chamber and its         2303900100031 
            diameter was of 6.1(1) cm, less than the diameter of  2303900100032 
            the 235-U deposits and than the diameter of 208Pb     2303900100033 
            sample.                                               2303900100034 
INC-SPECT  White neutron source from 2.6 to 20 MeV. Neutron energy2303900100035 
            (center of the energy bin) and uncertainty on neutron 2303900100036 
            energy as full width of the energy bin are coded under2303900100037 
            EN and EN-RSL-FW, respectively.                       2303900100038 
SAMPLE     Vacuum evaporated deposits, with a total areal density 2303900100039 
            of 3.066(6)mg/cm2. The chamber had 5 layers, 3 two-   2303900100040 
            sided and 2 one-sided.                                2303900100041 
           (82-PB-208,ENR=0.88110)                                2303900100042 
           (82-PB-206,ENR=0.10988)                                2303900100043 
           (82-PB-207,ENR=0.008943)                               2303900100044 
           (82-PB-204,ENR=0.0000758)                              2303900100045 
           Radiogenic 208Pb metallic sample with a mass of        2303900100046 
            217.45 g, diameter of 69.9(1) mm and thickness of     2303900100047 
            5.04 mm. Isotopic content: 88.110(63)% 208Pb,         2303900100048 
            10.988(64)% 206Pb, 0.8943(84)% 207Pb, 0.00758(45)%    2303900100049 
            204Pb.                                                2303900100050 
           The sample diameter was larger than the beam diameter. 2303900100051 
           (92-U-235,ENR=0.99826)                                 2303900100052 
           (92-U-234,ENR=0.00062)                                 2303900100053 
           (92-U-236,ENR=0.00036)                                 2303900100054 
           (92-U-237,ENR=0.00073)                                 2303900100055 
           The isotopic composition of the uranium deposits was   2303900100056 
            99.826(8)% 235U, 0.062(8)% 234U, 0.036(5)% 236U, and  2303900100057 
            0.073(9)% 237U.                                       2303900100058 
METHOD     (TOF) Time-of-flight with a 198.551m flight path. The  2303900100059 
            resolution was 8 ns time-of-flight which corresponds  2303900100060 
            to 1.12keV at 1 MeV and 35.7 keV at 10 MeV.           2303900100061

MONIT-REF  (,M.Sowerby,R,INDC(SEC)-101,51,1992)                   2303900100112 
DETECTOR   (HPGE) Two HPGe detectors and the fission chamber      2303900100113 
            recorded simultaneously. The time resolution of the   2303900100114 
            time coder was 0.5 ns. Conventional electronics was   2303900100115 
            used for both HPGe detectors and fission chamber and  2303900100116 
            the Constant Fraction Discriminators of the HPGe      2303900100117 
            detectors were set up on Slow Rise Time Rejection     2303900100118 
            function. The efficiencies were measured with a       2303900100119 
            standard point-like source of 152Eu of 3.1E+4Bq,      2303900100120 
            using samples of 56Co and 24Na produced by neutron    2303900100121 
            activation.                                           2303900100122 
           Four large volume HPGe detectors, with closed-ended    2303900100123 
            coaxial geometry. The relative efficiencies at        2303900100124 
            1.33 MeV and the distances from the sample position   2303900100125 
            to the detectors were:                                2303900100126 
            ---------------------------------------------------   2303900100127 
             Detector     Angle   Rel.-Efficiency     Distance    2303900100128 
            ---------------------------------------------------   2303900100129 
             1            110      75.9%              13.65 cm    2303900100130 
             2            150     104.3%              14.65 cm    2303900100131 
             3            110     105%                14.2 cm     2303900100132 
             4            150      98%                14.65 cm    2303900100133 
            ---------------------------------------------------   2303900100134 
            The energy resolution was around 2.4 keV at 1.332MeV. 2303900100135 
           (FISCH) The neutron flux was measured with a multilayer2303900100136 
            235U fission chamber. The fission chamber was used    2303900100137 
            without any change during the measurement campaign    2303900100138 
            that included 52Cr, 209Bi, 208Pb, 207Pb and 206Pb.    2303900100139 
            The shape of the neutron flux did not change during   2303900100140 
            this campaign.                                        2303900100141 
ANALYSIS   The differential gamma production cross-sections at    2303900100142 
            110 and respectively 150 degrees were derived         2303900100143 
            normalising point by point the HPGe yield to the 235U 2303900100144 
            fission chamber yield and to the 235U(n,f) cross      2303900100145 
            section.                                              2303900100146 
CORRECTION The following corrections were done:                   2303900100147 
            - Multiplication of original data (BgNS Transactions  2303900100148 
              10(2005)85, EUR 22343) by 0.875 (EUR 25208, Phys.   2303900100149 
              Rev.C91(2015)064618) to correct for fission chamber 2303900100150 
              efficiency redetermination.                         2303900100151 
            - Correction for the distance between positions of    2303900100152 
              the 208Pb sample and the position of the fission    2303900100153 
              chamber;                                            2303900100154 
            - Gamma-ray detection efficiency: extended volume     2303900100155 
              source and self-attenuation of the gamma rays in    2303900100156 
              the 208Pb sample means of MCNP (ver.4c2)            2303900100157 
              simulations. The HPGe efficiencies were corrected   2303900100158 
              for the coincident gamma rays from the 152Eu source.2303900100159 
              This correction was about 1%;                       2303900100160 
            - For the angular distribution: Gauss quadrature;     2303900100161 
            - For multiple scattering and attenuation of the      2303900100162 
              neutron beam in the 208Pb sample. This was done     2303900100163 
              with MCNP (ver.4c2) simulations;                    2303900100164 
            - No acquisition dead time was observed. To avoid the 2303900100165 
              possible dead time introduced in the HPGe detectors 2303900100166 
              acquisition system by the pile-up between the       2303900100167 
              neutron induced events and the gamma-flash induced  2303900100168 
              events;                                             2303900100169 
            - For the isotopic composition of the 208Pb sample;   2303900100170 
            - The 208Pb(n,2ng) and 208Pb(n,3ng) cross-sections    2303900100171 
              were corrected for the contribution of the (n,xng)  2303900100172 
              reactions on 207Pb and 206Pb. The (n,xng) cross     2303900100173 
              sections for 207Pb and 206Pb measured during the    2303900100174 
              same campaign. See  L.C.Mihailescu Ph.D. thesis.    2303900100175 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) Total uncertainties for the cross sections     2303900100176 
            were deduced by combining partial uncertainties from  2303900100177 
            various sources in quadrature. Uncertainty sources    2303900100178 
            considered were:                                      2303900100179 
           - 235U(n,f)cross-section uncertainties are point       2303900100180 
             dependent and are given above together with the      2303900100181 
             235U(n,f) cross-sections values                      2303900100182 
           (ERR-1,2.3,5.) HPGe efficiencies uncertainties were    2303900100183 
            almost the same for the two detectors, ranging from   2303900100184 
            2.3% at 0.4 MeV up to about 5% at 2.6 MeV gamma ray   2303900100185 
            energy.                                               2303900100186 
           (ERR-2) Fission chamber efficiency uncertainty was     2303900100187 
            1.16%;                                                2303900100188 
           (ERR-S,1.4,3.) Statistical counting uncertainties for  2303900100189 
            HPGe detectors and fission chamber are point          2303900100190 
            dependent. The statistical counting uncertainties of  2303900100191 
            the fission chamber yield range from about 1.4% at    2303900100192 
            2 MeV up to about 3% at 18 MeV.                       2303900100193 
COVARIANCE The analytical expressions employed are detailed in    2303900100194 
            the above mentioned NIM paper. Together with the list 2303900100195 
            of uncertainties on the quantities in these           2303900100196 
            expressions listed above this will allow the          2303900100197 
            evaluator to construct the covariance matrix. See     2303900100198 
            F.Froehner, JEFF report 18, OECD-NEA, Paris (2000);   2303900100199 
            and D.L.Smith, Neutron Physics and Nuclear Data in    2303900100200 
            Science and Technology, Vol.4, OECD-NEA, Paris (1991).2303900100201

             We used a value of 0.984(16) as the fission chamber  2303900100203

             0.875(10). See p55 of EUR 25208 EN for these values. 2303900100206
